The one where you said the gurl was knitting, she was crocheting. Knitting is making a ton of knots with two knitting 2 needles to create things such socks and blankets, crocheting is using a hook to create knot like texture on things like blankets, socks, ect. Finger knitting is using Esther 2-4 fingers and using yarn in a specific pattern depending on the amount of fingers to create a long, finger knitted thing that you can finger knit again to make thicker. Thatâ€™s all I know of knitting, finger knitting, and crocheting   A way to easily tell the difference is to look for knitting needles or the hook. Knitting creates a v like shape and crocheting can create more textures
